module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

endmodule

original text:  // You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd inst1 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4)
            begin : adder
                bcd_fadd inst (a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], carry[i-4], carry[i], sum[i+3:i]);
            end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];

endmodule

// You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [3:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd fadd1 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4) begin : adder
            bcd_fadd fadd (a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], carry[i-4], carry[i], sum[i+3:i]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[399];

endmodule

//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors)

module bcd_fadd (

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [3:0] c;
    bcd_fadd inst1 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, c[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4) begin : adder
            bcd_fadd inst (a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], c[i-4], c[i-3], sum[i+3:i]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = c[399];

endmodule

original text:  // You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd fadd0 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4) begin : adder
            bcd_fadd fadd (a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], carry[i-4], carry[i], sum[i+3:i]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];

endmodule

original text:  // You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    assign top_module.cout = bcd_fadd(a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, top_module.cout, top_module.sum[3:0]);
    assign top_module.sum[399:4] = a[399:4] + b[399:4] + top_module.cout;

endmodule

// You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    assign top_module.cout = bcd_fadd(a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, top_module.cout, top_module.sum[3:0]);
    assign top_module.sum[399:4] = a[399:4] + b[399:4] + top_module.cout;

endmodule

module bcd_fadd (

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [3:0] carry;
    
    genvar i;
    generate
        for (i=0; i<100; i=i+1) begin: adder
            bcd_fadd fa (
               .a(a[3*i+:3]),
               .b(b[3*i+:3]),
               .cin(carry[i]),
               .cout(carry[i+1]),
               .sum(sum[3*i+:3])
            );
        end
    endgenerate
    
    assign cout = carry[100];
    
endmodule

//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    bcd_fadd inst_fadd0 (
      .a(a[3:0]),
      .b(b[3:0]),
      .cin(cin),
      .cout(cout[0]),
      .sum(sum[3:0])
    );
    
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4) begin: adder
            bcd_fadd inst_fadd (
              .a(a[i+3:i]),
              .b(b[i+3:i]),
              .cin(cout[i-4]),
              .cout(cout[i]),
              .sum(sum[i+3:i])
            );
        end
    endgenerate

endmodule

original text:  // You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd fadd1 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4)
            assign carry[i/4] = (i/4 == 1)? carry[i/4-1] :
                                (i/4 == 2)? carry[i/4-2] :
                                (i/4 == 3)? carry[i/4-3] : 0;
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];

endmodule

// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd fadd_0 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4)
            assign carry[i/4] = carry[i/4] + a[i] & b[i];
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];

endmodule

// You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd fadd_0 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4)
            assign carry[i/4] = carry[i/4] + a[i] & b[i];
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];

endmodule

//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors)

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,

    bcd_fadd fadd1 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);

original text:  // You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    genvar i;
    generate
        for (i=0; i<100; i=i+1) begin
            bcd_fadd f(a[3*i+:3], b[3*i+:3], cin, carry[i], sum[3*i+:3]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[100];

endmodule

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.

original text:  // You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    genvar i;
    generate
        for (i=0; i<100; i=i+1) begin
            bcd_fadd f(a[3*i+:3], b[3*i+:3], cin, carry[i], sum[3*i+:3]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[100];
    
endmodule

original text:  // You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd inst1 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4) begin : adder
            bcd_fadd inst (a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], carry[i-4], carry[i], sum[i+3:i]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];

endmodule

    output   cout,

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [3:0] c;
    bcd_fadd f1 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, c[0], sum[3:0]);
    bcd_fadd f2 (a[7:4], b[7:4], c[0], c[1], sum[7:4]);
    bcd_fadd f3 (a[11:8], b[11:8], c[1], c[2], sum[11:8]);

    bcd_fadd f5 (a[19:16], b[19:16], c[3], cout, sum[19:16]);
    
endmodule

original text:  // You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    genvar i;
    generate
        for (i=0; i<100; i=i+1)
            full_adder fa (
               .a(a[i*4+3:i*4]),
               .b(b[i*4+3:i*4]),
               .cin(carry[i]),
               .cout(carry[i+1]),
               .sum(sum[i*4+3:i*4])
            );
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[100];

endmodule

//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    bcd_fadd fadd0(a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [3:0] c;
    bcd_fadd fadd1 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, cout, sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i=4; i<400; i=i+4) begin: adder
            bcd_fadd fadd (a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], cout, c[i/4], sum[i+3:i]);
        end
    endgenerate

endmodule

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] c;
    bcd_fadd inst1 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, c[0], sum[3:0]);

            end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = c[99];

// You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [3:0] c;
    bcd_fadd f1(a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, c[0], sum[3:0]);
    bcd_fadd f2(a[7:4], b[7:4], c[0], c[1], sum[7:4]);
    bcd_fadd f3(a[11:8], b[11:8], c[1], c[2], sum[11:8]);
    bcd_fadd f4(a[15:12], b[15:12], c[2], c[3], sum[15:12]);
    bcd_fadd f5(a[19:16], b[19:16], c[3], cout, sum[19:16]);
    
endmodule

module bcd_fadd (

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd inst_fadd (
       .a(a[3:0]),
       .b(b[3:0]),
       .cin(cin),
       .cout(carry[0]),
       .sum(sum[3:0])
    );
    genvar i;
    generate
        for (i=4; i<400; i=i+4) begin : adder
            bcd_fadd inst_fadd (
               .a(a[i+3:i]),
               .b(b[i+3:i]),
               .cin(carry[i-4]),
               .cout(carry[i]),
               .sum(sum[i+3:i])
            );
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];
    
endmodule

// You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [3:0] c;
    bcd_fadd inst_fadd0 (
      .a(a[3:0]),
      .b(b[3:0]),
      .cin(cin),
      .cout(c[0]),
      .sum(sum[3:0])
    );
    
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4) begin : adder
            bcd_fadd inst_fadd (
              .a(a[i+3:i]),
              .b(b[i+3:i]),
              .cin(c[i-4]),
              .cout(c[i]),
              .sum(sum[i+3:i])
            );
        end
    endgenerate
    
    assign cout = c[399];

endmodule

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd fadd_0 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4) begin : adder
            bcd_fadd fadd_temp (a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], carry[i-4], carry[i], sum[i+3:i]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];

endmodule

//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors)

    input [399:0] a, b,

    output cout,

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    assign cout = (a[399] == b[399])? cin : 0;
    assign sum = a + b;

module bcd_fadd (

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd fadd0 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4) begin : adder
            bcd_fadd fadd (a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], carry[i-4], carry[i], sum[i+3:i]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];

endmodule

original text:  // You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd fadd_0 (
       .a(a[3:0]),
       .b(b[3:0]),
       .cin(cin),
       .cout(carry[0]),
       .sum(sum[3:0])
    );
    
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i=1; i<100; i=i+1) begin: adder
            bcd_fadd fadd_i (
               .a(a[(4*i)+3:4*i]),
               .b(b[(4*i)+3:4*i]),
               .cin(carry[i-1]),
               .cout(carry[i]),
               .sum(sum[(4*i)+3:4*i])
            );
        end
    endgenerate
    
    assign cout = carry[99];
    
endmodule

    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );

//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors)

// You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [3:0] c;
    bcd_fadd a1(a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, c[0], sum[3:0]);
    bcd_fadd a2(a[7:4], b[7:4], c[0], c[1], sum[7:4]);
    bcd_fadd a3(a[11:8], b[11:8], c[1], c[2], sum[11:8]);
    bcd_fadd a4(a[15:12], b[15:12], c[2], c[3], sum[15:12]);
    bcd_fadd a5(a[19:16], b[19:16], c[3], cout, sum[19:16]);
    
endmodule

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd fadd_0 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4) begin : adder
            bcd_fadd fadd_temp(a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], carry[i-4], carry[i], sum[i+3:i]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];

endmodule

// You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [3:0] c;
    bcd_fadd fadd1 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, c[0], sum[3:0]);
    bcd_fadd fadd2 (a[7:4], b[7:4], c[0], c[1], sum[7:4]);
    bcd_fadd fadd3 (a[11:8], b[11:8], c[1], c[2], sum[11:8]);
    bcd_fadd fadd4 (a[15:12], b[15:12], c[2], c[3], sum[15:12]);
    bcd_fadd fadd5 (a[19:16], b[19:16], c[3], cout, sum[19:16]);
    
endmodule

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    genvar i;
    generate
        for (i=0; i<100; i=i+1) begin: adder
            bcd_fadd f(a[3*i+:3], b[3*i+:3], carry[i], carry[i+1], sum[3*i+:3]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[100];

endmodule

// You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] c;
    bcd_fadd fadd_0 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, c[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for(i=1;i<100;i=i+1) begin: adder
            bcd_fadd fadd_i (a[(4*i)+3:4*i], b[(4*i)+3:4*i], c[i-1], c[i], sum[(4*i)+3:4*i]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = c[99];
    
endmodule

// You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd inst_fadd (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4) begin : adder
            bcd_fadd inst_fadd (a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], carry[i-4], carry[i], sum[i+3:i]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];

endmodule

// You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd inst_fadd (
      .a(a[3:0]),
      .b(b[3:0]),
      .cin(cin),
      .cout(carry[0]),
      .sum(sum[3:0])
    );
    genvar i;
    generate
        for (i=4; i<400; i=i+4) begin: adder
            bcd_fadd inst_fadd (
              .a(a[i+3:i]),
              .b(b[i+3:i]),
              .cin(carry[i-4]),
              .cout(carry[i]),
              .sum(sum[i+3:i])
            );
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];

endmodule

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    genvar i;
    generate
        for (i=0; i<100; i=i+1) begin: adder
            bcd_fadd fa (
               .a(a[3*i+:3]),
               .b(b[3*i+:3]),
               .cin(carry[i]),
               .cout(carry[i+1]),
               .sum(sum[3*i+:3])
            );
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[100];

endmodule

original text:  // You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd inst_fadd (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4) begin : adder
            bcd_fadd inst_fadd (a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], carry[i-4], carry[i], sum[i+3:i]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];

endmodule

original text:  // You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [3:0] c;
    bcd_fadd f1 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, c[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4) begin : adder
            bcd_fadd f (a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], c[i-4], c[i-3], sum[i+3:i]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = c[399];

endmodule

// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd fadd0 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4)
            assign carry[i/4] = (a[i] & b[i]) | (a[i] & carry[i-4]) | (b[i] & carry[i-4]);
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];

endmodule

// You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] c;
    bcd_fadd fadd0 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, c[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4)
            begin : adder
                bcd_fadd fadd (a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], c[i-4], c[i], sum[i+3:i]);
            end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = c[99];

endmodule

original text:  // You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd fadd0(a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4) begin : adder
            bcd_fadd fadd(a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], carry[i-4], carry[i], sum[i+3:i]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];

endmodule

// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd fadd_0(a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4) begin
            bcd_fadd fadd_temp(a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], carry[i-4], carry[i], sum[i+3:i]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];

endmodule

//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors)

module top_module(

// You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] c;
    bcd_fadd inst1 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, c[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4)
            begin : adder
                bcd_fadd inst (a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], c[i-4], c[i], sum[i+3:i]);
            end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = c[99];

endmodule

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    genvar i;
    generate
        for(i=0; i<100; i=i+1) begin
            bcd_fadd f(a[3*i+:3], b[3*i+:3], cin, carry[i], sum[3*i+:3]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[100];

endmodule

// You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    genvar i;
    generate
        for(i=0; i<100; i=i+1) begin
            bcd_fadd f(a[3*i+:3], b[3*i+:3], cin, carry[i], sum[3*i+:3]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[100];

endmodule

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    bcd_fadd inst_fadd0 (
      .a(a[3:0]),
      .b(b[3:0]),
      .cin(cin),
      .cout(cout[0]),
      .sum(sum[3:0])
    );
    
    generate
        genvar i;
        for(i=1;i<400;i=i+1) begin: adder
            bcd_fadd inst_fadd(
              .a(a[(i*4)-1:(i-1)*4]),
              .b(b[(i*4)-1:(i-1)*4]),
              .cin(cout[i-1]),
              .cout(cout[i]),
              .sum(sum[(i*4)-1:(i-1)*4])
            );
        end
    endgenerate

endmodule

// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    genvar i;
    generate
        for(i=0;i<100;i=i+1) begin
            bcd_fadd fadd(a[3*i+:3],b[3*i+:3],carry[i],carry[i+1],sum[3*i+:3]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[100];
    
endmodule

//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors)

// You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    bcd_fadd fadd_0(a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, carry[0], sum[3:0]);
    generate
        genvar i;
        for (i = 4; i < 400; i = i + 4) begin
            bcd_fadd fadd_i(a[i+3:i], b[i+3:i], carry[i-4], carry[i], sum[i+3:i]);
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[99];

endmodule

// You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [3:0] c;
    bcd_fadd fadd1 (a[3:0], b[3:0], cin, c[0], sum[3:0]);
    bcd_fadd fadd2 (a[7:4], b[7:4], c[0], c[1], sum[7:4]);

endmodule

original text:  // You are provided with a BCD one-digit adder named bcd_fadd that adds 
// two BCD digits and carry-in, and produces a sum and carry-out.

module bcd_fadd (
    input [3:0] a,
    input [3:0] b,
    input     cin,
    output   cout,
    output [3:0] sum );
    
// Instantiate 100 copies of bcd_fadd to create a 100-digit BCD ripple-carry adder. 
//Your adder should add two 100-digit BCD numbers (packed into 400-bit vectors) 
//and a carry-in to produce a 100-digit sum and carry out.


// Hint: An instance array or generate statement would be useful here.

module top_module( 
    input [399:0] a, b,
    input cin,
    output cout,
    output [399:0] sum );

    wire [99:0] carry;
    genvar i;
    generate
        for (i=0; i<100; i=i+1) begin: adder
            bcd_fadd fa (
               .a(a[3*i+:3]),
               .b(b[3*i+:3]),
               .cin(carry[i]),
               .cout(carry[i+1]),
               .sum(sum[3*i+:3])
            );
        end
    endgenerate
    assign cout = carry[100];

endmodule
